  Reading: fluid conduit line.
  Confidence: strong

### Game Theory

- `L.1`
  Equation:

  \[y_{\mathrm{L_1}}^+ = \operatorname*{argmin}_{y \in \Delta(\mathcal{A})}\{R_{\mathrm{L_1}}(y) + \lambda_{\mathrm{L_1}} C(y, y_{\mathrm{L_1}}^-)\}\]

  Variable legend: `y` is the strategy distribution; `R_line` is risk and `C` the control-cost.
  Reading: fluid conduit line.
  Confidence: strong

  Equation:

## Direct Operational Meaning

A full bathhouse state-machine: name the ports, run oscillation (work ↔ settle) until the system can support two explicit commits, then finish by collapsing the whole network into a single sealed terminal state. Process statistics: 96 circulation commands (qo-); 12 valve/clamp checkpoints (ckh/kch); 24 infusion-stabilize cycles (shedy); 7 completion markers (daiin); 3 salt/crystallization references (sal).

## Mathematical Extraction

Across the formal lenses, `f77v` behaves as a fixed-point purification page with N_qo=67, N_valve=8, and N_seal=1. The governing update is x_(n+1) = V(C(x_n)); stop when ||x_(n+1)-x_n|| <= eps, then publish y = S(x_*).

## Mythic Extraction

`f77v` is a bathhouse-laboratory chamber: descend through linked pools, purify by circulation, prove stability at the clamps, and only then carry the living fluid onward.

## All-Lens Zero Point

`A full bathhouse state-machine: name the ports, run oscillation (work ↔ settle) until the system can support two explicit commits, then finish by collapsing the whole network into a single sealed terminal state.`

\[g = \mathrm{Coll}(X), \qquad X = \mathrm{Expand}(g) \oplus r\]

### Typed State Machine

\[
\mathcal R_{f77v} = \{r_{charge}, r_{circulate}, r_{clamp}, r_{commit}, r_{seal}\}
\]
\[
\delta(r_{charge})=r_{circulate}, \qquad
\delta(r_{circulate})=r_{clamp}, \qquad
\delta(r_{clamp})=
\begin{cases}
r_{circulate} & \text{if } \Delta_n > 0 \\
r_{commit} & \text{if } \Delta_n = 0
\end{cases}
\]
\[
\delta(r_{commit})=
\begin{cases}
r_{seal} & \text{if } P_{salt} = 1 \\
r_{circulate} & \text{otherwise}
\end{cases}
\]
